The hotel is children friendly and have numerous activities for the young visitors including a separate dedicated venue for them. There was no handrail to support the ground with my hands. My wrist was swollen and my hips were in unbearable pain. It was around 3 pm at this time. There was no service staff by the pool. I took a short break and reluctantly walked to the front desk. The little sister gave me Panax notoginseng spray, which relieved a little.
So it is recommended that the hotel install handrails by the pool to ensure the safety of tourists entering the water, otherwise it will be troublesome if they fall and fracture. Thanks to the little sister at the front desk for providing the medicine in time.
